option).\n40:  * <p>\n41:  * Depending on the barrier defined in {@link Barrier}, the options are classified into four types: up-and-in,\n42:  * down-and-in, up-and-out and down-and-out.\n43:  * <p>\n44:  * For example, an up-and-out call on a 'EUR 1.00 / USD -1.41' exchange with barrier of 1.5 is the option to\n45:  * perform a foreign exchange on the expiry date, where USD 1.41 is paid to
